### [334] [Meta-Ensemble Learning with Diverse Data Splits for Improved Respiratory Sound Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24096)
*June-Woo Kim,Miika Toikkanen,Heejoon Koo,Yoon Tae Kim,Doyoung Kwon,Kyunghoon Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种元集成学习方法，通过在不同数据划分和粒度设置下训练基模型，以增强预测多样性，并利用训练好的元模型融合输出。该方法在ICBHI基准上达到66.49%的得分，创下新纪录，并在两个分布外数据集上表现出更好的泛化能力，表明其在真实临床数据中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有呼吸音分类模型受限于数据集规模小和受试者多样性不足，且传统集成方法因基模型使用相同数据而产生高相关性预测，降低集成效果。

Method: 在ICBHI数据集上采用固定80-20%划分与五折交叉验证两种数据划分方式，以及患者级和样本级两种数据粒度，训练多个基模型；通过训练一个元模型来融合这些基模型的输出，以提升预测多样性与泛化能力。

Result: 在ICBHI基准上取得66.49%的得分，为当前最优性能；在两个分布外数据集上表现更优，证明了模型良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的元集成学习方法有效提升了基模型预测的多样性，显著增强了模型在真实临床场景下的泛化能力，具有实际应用前景。

Abstract: Training reliable respiratory sound classification models remains challenging due to the limited size and subject diversity of datasets. Ensemble methods can improve robustness, but when base models are trained on identical data, models tend to overfit and produce highly correlated predictions, thereby reducing the effectiveness of ensembling. In this work, we investigate a meta-ensemble learning methodology that enhances prediction diversity by training base models on diverse data splits and combining their outputs through a trained meta-model. Specifically, we train base models on the ICBHI dataset using two data split settings: fixed 80-20% split and five-fold cross-validation split, under two data granularity settings: patient- and sample-level. The resulting diversity in base model predictions enables the meta-model to better generalize. Our approach achieves new state-of-the-art performance on the ICBHI benchmark, reaching a Score of 66.49% and showing improved generalization on two out-of-distribution datasets, indicating its potential applicability to real-world clinical data.

### [335] [Fed-DLoRA: Efficient Wireless Federated Learning with Dynamic Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24103)
*Huaicheng Li,Junhui Zhao,Haoyu Quan,Xiaoming Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种轻量级联邦学习算法Fed-DLoRA，结合低秩适应（LoRA）技术以减少参数和通信开销，同时提升训练效率。通过随机梯度下降与奇异值分解的收敛性分析，揭示了LoRA秩、车辆调度策略与模型收敛特性之间的理论关系，并设计了联合优化问题。为此提出了自适应秩、带宽与车辆选择（ARBVS）算法，融合枚举与贪婪优化策略，实现每轮通信中的高效秩选择与资源调度，显著提升了系统性能。实验表明，相比传统方法，该方法在准确率、收敛速度和通信效率方面均有明显优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决车联网中联邦学习面临的通信开销大、环境动态变化等问题，同时克服模型压缩带来的压缩比与车辆参与策略之间的权衡难题。

Method: 提出Fed-DLoRA算法，结合低秩适应（LoRA）技术，利用随机梯度下降与奇异值分解进行收敛性分析，并设计基于枚举与贪婪优化的自适应秩、带宽与车辆选择（ARBVS）算法，实现高效资源调度与模型优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，Fed-DLoRA在准确率、收敛速度和通信效率方面均优于传统联邦学习方法，显著提升了系统整体性能。

Conclusion: Fed-DLoRA通过引入低秩适应机制与自适应资源调度策略，在降低通信与计算负担的同时保障了模型性能，为车联网场景下的高效联邦学习提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) offers a promising distributed learning paradigm for internet of vehicles (IoV) applications. However, it faces challenges from communication overhead and dynamic environments. Model compression techniques reduce computing and communication burden yet create trade-offs between compression ratios and vehicle participation strategies. In this paper, we propose a lightweight FL algorithm named federated learning with dynamic low-rank adaptation (Fed-DLoRA), which is combined with low-rank adaptation (LoRA) to effectively reduce parameters and communication costs while enhancing training efficiency. The convergence analysis of Fed-DLoRA is conducted through stochastic gradient descent optimization coupled with singular value decomposition. This analysis establishes the theoretical relationships among LoRA rank, vehicular scheduling strategies and the model's convergence characteristics. Building on these insights, we formulate a joint optimization problem aimed at maximizing system performance. To address this problem, we propose an adaptive rank, bandwidth and vehicle selection (ARBVS) algorithm that integrates enumeration with greedy optimization strategies. The algorithm provides efficient rank selection and resource scheduling strategies for each FL communication round, thereby achieving effective performance improvements for the FL system. Experimental results demonstrate that Fed-DLoRA achieves superior performance compared to conventional federated learning approaches, exhibiting enhanced accuracy, faster convergence, and improved communication efficiency.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Based on semantic labelling, we propose Semantically Relevant Skill Discovery (SRSD), a novel human-in-the-loop approach that collects semantic labels from human feedback and learns a reward function to encourage skills to be more semantically diverse and relevant. ### [337] [CMGL: Confidence-guided Multi-omics Graph Learning for Cancer Subtype Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24201)

Method: 提出CMGL框架，第一阶段使用证据深度学习估计每个样本各模态的可靠性；第二阶段冻结这些置信度得分，用于指导跨组学融合与图构建。

  Results: We propose CMGL, a two-stage framework that estimates per-sample modality reliability through evidential deep learning and uses the frozen confidence scores to guide cross-omics fusion and graph construction. On four MLOmics cancer-subtype tasks and the 32-class pan-cancer task, CMGL consistently improves over the strongest baseline, surpassing it by 4.03% in average accuracy on the four single-cancer tasks. Its representations recover the PAM50 intrinsic subtypes of breast invasive carcinoma (BRCA), and the BRCA-trained model transfers without fine-tuning to kidney renal clear cell carcinoma (KIRC), stratifying patients into prognostically distinct groups.

### [338] [IMPA-Net: Meteorology-Aware Multi-Scale Attention and Dynamic Loss for Extreme Convective Radar Nowcasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24224)
*Haofei Cui,Guangxin He,Juanzhen Sun,Jingjia Luo,Haonan Chen,Xiaoran Zhuang,Mingxuan Chen,Xian Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: IMPA-Net 是一种用于0-2小时对流降水短时预报的确定性框架，通过气象学启发的设计在输入、架构和损失函数层面解决深度学习模型过度平滑、多尺度特征交互不足及异质地理输入融合不佳的问题。其核心包括：参数无关的空间混合器（Spatial Mixer）在~2公里中尺度区域进行通道重排以提供结构化跨场先验；集成多尺度预测注意力模块捕捉从β到γ中尺度的动力学；以及气象感知动态损失函数，采用三层次非对称加权（训练周期、风暴强度、预报时效）对抗回归均值现象。在华东地区多源雷达数据集上评估，相较于七种基线，IMPA-Net将≥45 dBZ的海德克技能得分从0.049提升至0.143；相比pySTEPS，在严重事件检测与误报控制间取得更优平衡。谱分析显示其在中尺度能量带保持能力优于竞争方法，避免了渐进性平滑。但当前结果仅在单一地形与对流气候条件下验证，泛化性仍待检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习模型在对流降水短时预报中因使用像素级误差指标，常生成过于平滑的预报结果，抑制了关键强回波信号，影响灾害预警效果。同时存在多尺度特征交互不足和异质地理输入融合不充分的问题，亟需引入气象学先验知识改进模型设计。

Method: 提出IMPA-Net框架，包含三个核心组件：1）参数无关的空间混合器（Spatial Mixer），在~2公里中尺度邻域内通过确定性通道置换重组异质输入通道，提供结构化跨场先验；2）集成多尺度预测注意力模块，作为时空翻译器，捕获从mesoscale-β到mesoscale-γ尺度的动力学信息；3）气象感知动态损失函数，采用三层次非对称权重机制（随训练周期、风暴强度、预报时效自适应调整），缓解回归均值问题。

Result: 在华东地区多源雷达数据集上，IMPA-Net在≥45 dBZ的预报中，海德克技能得分由基线SimVP的0.049提升至0.143（相同设置下）；相较于pySTEPS，在严重天气事件检测能力与误报率控制之间表现更优。谱分析证实该模型在中尺度能量频段保留能力更强，未出现其他方法中的渐进性平滑现象。

Conclusion: IMPA-Net通过气象学启发的输入、架构与损失函数设计，有效提升了对流降水短时预报中强回波的保真度与检测能力，显著改善了预报质量。然而，该方法目前仅在一个对流主导的地理区域内验证，其在不同地形与气候条件下的泛化性能尚需进一步测试。

Abstract: Short-range prediction of convective precipitation from weather radar observations is essential for severe weather warnings. However, deep learning models trained with pixel-wise error metrics tend to produce overly smooth forecasts that suppress intense echoes critical for hazard detection. This issue is exacerbated by insufficient multi-scale feature interaction and suboptimal fusion of heterogeneous geophysical inputs. We propose IMPA-Net (Integrated Multi-scale Predictive Attention Network), a deterministic 0-2 hour nowcasting framework that addresses these limitations through meteorologically-informed designs at the input, architecture, and loss function levels. A parameter-free Spatial Mixer reorganizes heterogeneous input channels at the mesoscale-$γ$ neighborhood (~2 km) via deterministic channel permutation, providing a structured cross-field prior. An integrated multi-scale predictive attention module serves as the spatiotemporal translator, capturing dynamics from mesoscale-$β$ to mesoscale-$γ$ scales. A Meteorologically-Aware Dynamic Loss employs three-level asymmetric weighting -- adapting across training epochs, storm intensity, and forecast lead time -- to counteract regression-to-the-mean. Evaluated against seven baselines on a multi-source radar dataset over eastern China, IMPA-Net raises the Heidke Skill Score at $\geq$45 dBZ from 0.049 (SimVP baseline) to 0.143 under matched settings. Relative to pySTEPS, it provides a better trade-off between severe-event detection and false-alarm control. Spectral analysis confirms preserved energy across mesoscale bands where competing methods show progressive smoothing. These improvements are shown within a single domain and convective regime; generalizability to other orographic and climatic regions remains to be tested.

</details>


### [339] [GeoEdit: Local Frames for Fast, Training-Free On-Manifold Editing in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24238)
*Yiming Zhang,Sitong Liu,Ke Li,Zhihong Wu,Alex Cloninger,Melvin Leok*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种无需训练的扩散模型编辑方法，通过在数据流形附近进行局部更新，避免重复完整的去噪过程。利用扰动样本估计流形切空间，并证明其接近真实切空间；基于此设计了一种无雅可比矩阵的算法，通过初始噪声的小扰动构建切空间基，并交替执行切向移动与扩散投影。该方法在流形上保持语义一致性，支持快速、连续的编辑调整，且不依赖额外训练，可直接集成到现有采样器中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统训练-free 扩散模型编辑需为每次编辑强度重新运行完整去噪轨迹，导致迭代优化成本高昂。为提升效率，需要一种能在数据流形附近进行小规模局部更新的方法，以避免重复重生成。

Method: 通过扰动样本估计流形切空间，构建切向基；设计无雅可比矩阵的算法，结合小扰动生成切向移动和扩散投影，实现流形上的精细编辑。

Result: 实验表明，该方法能实现平滑、语义连贯的无监督遍历，支持有效的 CLIP 引导优化，具备实际交互式连续编辑能力，且保持高保真度。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了无需训练、高效、可插拔的连续编辑，显著降低计算开销，同时保证编辑质量，为扩散模型的交互式编辑提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion models are a leading paradigm for data generation, but training-free editing typically re-runs the full denoising trajectory for every edit strength, making iterative refinement expensive. To address this issue, we instead edit near the data manifold, where small local updates can replace repeated re-synthesis. To enable this, we estimate a local manifold tangent space directly from perturbed samples and prove that this sample-based estimator closely approximates the true tangent. Building on this guarantee, we devise a Jacobian-free algorithm that constructs a tangent frame via small perturbations to the initial noise and alternates small tangent moves with diffusion-based projections. Updates within this frame follow principled on-manifold directions while suppressing off-manifold drift, enabling fine-grained edits without full re-diffusion or additional training. Edit strength is controlled by the number of steps for rapid, continuous adjustments that preserve fidelity and plug into existing samplers. Empirically, the resulting tangent directions yield smooth, semantic unsupervised traversals and effective CLIP-guided optimization, demonstrating practical interactive continuous editing.

### [341] [Latent-Hysteresis Graph ODEs: Modeling Coupled Topology-Feature Evolution via Continuous Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24293)
*Qinhan Hou,Jing Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Hysteresis Graph ODE（HGODE），通过引入具有双阱边势能和双极化门的潜在拓扑动力学，解决传统图微分方程因正不可约混合算子导致的长期信息泄漏与单一致共识陷阱问题。该方法在保持可微性的同时实现边状态的极化，支持连接或绝缘相变，并在合成与真实世界图数据上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统图神经微分方程（Graph ODEs）虽支持自适应长程传播，但受限于严格正且不可约的混合算子，在长时间演化下不可避免地陷入单一致共识状态，导致信息丢失。亟需一种机制来打破这种单调稳定性，保留多样化的节点表示。

Method: 提出HGODE模型，将特征演化与由学习到的成对力驱动的潜在拓扑势耦合。采用双阱边势能和双极化门，使边状态能够极化为连通或绝缘两种相态，同时保证整体可微性。

Result: 理论分析揭示了原有图ODE的坍塌机制；实验表明HGODE在合成诊断任务和真实图基准上均有效缓解了信息衰减问题，提升了表示能力与泛化性能。

Conclusion: HGODE通过引入具有滞后的拓扑动态机制，成功突破了图微分方程的单一致共识限制，为连续时间图学习提供了更灵活、鲁棒的建模框架。

Abstract: Graph neural ordinary differential equations (Graph ODEs) extend graph learning from discrete message-passing layers to continuous-time representation flows. While it supports adaptive long-range propagation, we show that Graph ODEs with strictly positive irreducible mixing operators face an inherent \emph{monostability trap}: in the long-time regime, information leakage is unavoidable and the dynamics converge to a single global consensus attractor. We propose the \textbf{Hysteresis Graph ODE (HGODE)}, which couples feature evolution with a latent topological potential driven by a learned pairwise force. A double-well edge potential and bipolarized gate allow edge states to polarize into connected or insulated phases while preserving differentiability. We provide asymptotic analysis of the collapse mechanism and the proposed hysteretic topology dynamics, and validate HGODE on theory-driven synthetic diagnostics and real-world graph benchmarks.

It outperforms previous models, especially on varied weather conditions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurate short-term solar power forecasting is crucial for integrating renewable energy into the grid efficiently. Existing models struggle with capturing complex temporal dependencies and spatial variability in solar irradiance, particularly across different locations and weather conditions.

Method: SolarTformer uses a transformer-inspired architecture with self-attention mechanisms to process meteorological data and incorporates power station-specific metadata (e.g., location, panel configuration, season) to enhance model generalization.

Result: SolarTformer significantly outperforms prior models on the same dataset, demonstrating high accuracy and robustness on both clear and cloudy days, indicating strong adaptability across diverse conditions.

Conclusion: Attention-based deep learning architectures like SolarTformer show great promise in improving solar power forecasting accuracy, enabling more reliable and efficient renewable energy management.

Abstract: Accurate forecasting of solar power output is essential for efficient integration of renewable energy into the grid. In this study, an attention-based deep learning model, inspired by transformer architecture, is used for short-term solar power forecasting. Our proposed model, "SolarTformer", is designed to predict solar power output from meteorological data. Unlike traditional models, SolarTformer leverages self-attention mechanisms to effectively capture temporal dependencies and spatial variability in solar irradiance. In addition, the proposed methodology includes feeding power station-specific metadata into the model, which helps to generalize between power stations located at different locations and with different panel configurations and in different seasons. Our experiments demonstrate that SolarTformer significantly outperforms previous models on the same data set. In particular, the model exhibits strong performance on both clear and cloudy days, indicating high robustness and generalizability. These findings highlight the potential of attention-based architectures in enhancing the accuracy of solar forecasting, contributing to a more reliable management of renewable energy.

### [343] [Mitigating Error Amplification in Fast Adversarial Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24332)
*Mengnan Zhao,Lihe Zhang,Bo Wang,Tianhang Zheng,Hong Zhong,Geyong Min*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为分布感知动态引导（DDG）的新方法，旨在解决快速对抗训练（FAT）中的灾难性过拟合（CO）和鲁棒性与干净输入性能之间的权衡问题。通过分析不同置信度样本的影响，发现低置信度样本是导致上述问题的主要原因。DDG根据样本在真实类别上的置信度动态调整扰动幅度和监督信号，以促进一致决策边界并避免学习虚假相关性。同时引入加权正则化约束缓解梯度不稳定性。实验表明，DDG在多个标准基准上有效缓解了CO和性能下降问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速对抗训练虽能提升模型鲁棒性，但存在灾难性过拟合问题，且随着扰动预算增大，模型在干净数据上的性能显著下降。现有方法未能有效解决低置信度样本带来的负面影响。

Method: 提出分布感知动态引导（DDG）策略，动态调节扰动强度与监督信号：依据样本对真实类别的置信度调整扰动幅度；根据预测状态动态调整监督信号，并引入加权正则化以稳定梯度。

Result: 在多个标准数据集上的实验验证了DDG的有效性，能够显著缓解灾难性过拟合现象，并减轻鲁棒性与干净准确率之间的权衡，提升整体性能。

Conclusion: 通过分析置信度对训练过程的影响，提出DDG策略，实现了更稳健、更高效的对抗训练，为解决当前对抗训练中的核心挑战提供了新思路。

Abstract: Fast Adversarial Training (FAT) has proven effective in enhancing model robustness by encouraging networks to learn perturbation-invariant representations. However, FAT often suffers from catastrophic overfitting (CO), where the model overfits to the training attack and fails to generalize to unseen ones. Moreover, robustness oriented optimization typically leads to notable performance degradation on clean inputs, and such degradation becomes increasingly severe as the perturbation budget grows. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive analysis of how guidance strength affects model performance by modulating perturbation and supervision levels across distinct confidence groups. The findings reveal that low confidence samples are the primary contributors to CO and the robustness accuracy trade off. Building on this insight, we propose a Distribution-aware Dynamic Guidance (DDG) strategy that dynamically adjusts both the perturbation budget and supervision signal. Specifically, DDG scales the perturbation magnitude according to the sample confidence at the ground truth class, thereby guiding samples toward consistent decision boundaries while mitigating the influence of learning spurious correlations. Simultaneously, it dynamically adjusts the supervision signal based on the prediction state of each sample, preventing overemphasis on incorrect signals. To alleviate potential gradient instability arising from dynamic guidance, we further design a weighted regularization constraint. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that DDG effectively alleviates both CO and the robustness accuracy trade off.

### [344] [Unveiling the Backdoor Mechanism Hidden Behind Catastrophic Overfitting in Fast Adversarial Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24350)
*Mengnan Zhao,Lihe Zhang,Tianhang Zheng,Bo Wang,Baocai Yin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将快速对抗训练中的灾难性过拟合（CO）解释为后门攻击的一种弱变体，提出了一种统一的理论框架，将CO、后门攻击和不可学习任务联系起来，并基于此设计了两种缓解策略：参数重校准和权重异常抑制，实验验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法虽能缓解灾难性过拟合（CO），但缺乏系统且直观的解释，导致应对策略较为零散。本文旨在揭示CO的本质，提供统一的理论视角。

Method: 通过后门攻击的视角重新诠释CO，提出其为一种弱触发的不可学习任务；设计基于后门启发的缓解策略，包括使用常规微调、线性探测或重新初始化来重校准受影响的模型参数，以及引入权重异常抑制约束以控制模型权重的异常偏差。

Result: 实验结果表明，该理论解释合理，所提出的缓解策略能有效降低CO现象，提升模型在不同对抗攻击下的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文从后门攻击的角度揭示了灾难性过拟合的本质，建立了统一的理论框架，并提出了有效的缓解方法，为提升对抗训练的鲁棒性和泛化能力提供了新思路。

Abstract: Fast Adversarial Training (FAT) has attracted significant attention due to its efficiency in enhancing neural network robustness against adversarial attacks. However, FAT is prone to catastrophic overfitting (CO), wherein models overfit to the specific attack used during training and fail to generalize to others. While existing methods introduce diverse hypotheses and propose various strategies to mitigate CO, a systematic and intuitive explanation of CO remains absent. In this work, we innovatively interpret CO through the lens of backdoor. Through validations on pathway division, diverse feature predictions, and universal class distinguishable triggers in CO, we conceptualize CO as a weak trigger variant of unlearnable tasks, unifying CO, backdoor attacks, and unlearnable tasks under a common theoretical framework. Guided by this, we leverage several backdoor inspired strategies to mitigate CO: (i) Recalibrate CO affected model parameters using vanilla fine tuning, linear probing, or reinitialization-based techniques; (ii) Introduce a weight outlier suppression constraint to regulate abnormal deviations in model weights. Extensive experiments support our interpretation of CO and show the efficacy of the proposed mitigation strategies.

### [346] [DPRM: A Plug-in Doob h transform-induced Token-Ordering Module for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24357)
*Dake Bu,Wei Huang,Andi Han,Hau-San Wong,Qingfu Zhang,Taiji Suzuki,Atsushi Nitanda*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DPRM 是一种用于扩散语言模型的即插即用式标记排序模块，通过结合置信度驱动的渐进排序与 Doob h 变换过程奖励模型引导的排序，实现更优的生成策略。它在不改变原有架构和训练目标的前提下，优化了标记揭示顺序，在预训练、后训练、测试时扩展及单细胞掩码扩散任务中均优于基于置信度的基线方法，尤其在高难度推理子集上表现突出。在蛋白质、分子生成和 DNA 设计等多目标场景中，排序感知变体显著提升结构或片段约束指标，同时保持对整体质量的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散语言模型的标记排序方法主要依赖随机掩码或仅基于置信度的规则，前者导致训练-测试不一致，后者可能过于短视且抑制探索。因此需要一种既能避免偏差又能促进有效探索的新型排序机制。

Method: 提出 DPRM（Doob h-transform Process Reward Model），从置信度驱动的渐进排序出发，通过在线估计逐步过渡到由 Doob h 变换过程奖励模型引导的排序策略。该方法定义为奖励倾斜的 Gibbs 揭示律，并通过软 BoN 近似实现阶跃式收敛，同时使用分桶化控制器以经验伯恩斯坦速率跟踪精确得分。

Result: DPRM 在多个任务中超越置信度基线，尤其在复杂推理任务中优势明显；在蛋白质、分子生成和 DNA 设计中，排序感知版本显著改善结构或片段约束相关指标，虽未在所有质量指标上全面领先，但展现出更强的多目标优化能力。

Conclusion: 标记排序是扩散语言模型中的一个核心控制轴，DPRM 作为通用模块可有效提升其性能，具有广泛适用性和实际价值。代码已开源。

Abstract: Diffusion language models generate without a fixed left-to-right order, making token ordering a central algorithmic choice: which tokens should be revealed, retained, revised or verified at each step? Existing systems mainly use random masking or confidence-driven ordering. Random masking creates train--test mismatch, while confidence-only rules are efficient but can be myopic and suppress useful exploration.
  We introduce DPRM (Doob h-transform Process Reward Model), a plug-in token-ordering module for diffusion language models. DPRM keeps the host architecture, denoising objective and supervision unchanged, and changes only the ordering policy. It starts from confidence-driven progressive ordering and gradually shifts to Doob h transform Process Reward guided ordering through online estimates.
  We characterize the exact DPRM policy as a reward-tilted Gibbs reveal law, prove O(1/N) convergence of the stagewise Soft-BoN approximation, and show that the online bucketized controller tracks the exact DPRM score at empirical-Bernstein rates. Under tractable optimization assumptions, DPRM also yields a sample-complexity advantage over random and confidence-only ordering.
  DPRM improves over confidence-based baselines in pretraining, post-training, test-time scaling, and single-cell masked diffusion, with particularly strong gains on harder reasoning subsets. In protein, molecular generation and DNA design, the effect is more multi-objective: ordering-aware variants significantly improve selected structural or fragment-constrained metrics while not uniformly dominating the host baseline on every quality metric. These results identify token ordering as a fundamental control axis in diffusion language models and establish DPRM as a general-purpose module for improving it. Code is available at https://github.com/DakeBU/DPRM-DLLM.

</details>


### [347] [SAGE: Sparse Adaptive Guidance for Dependency-Aware Tabular Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24368)
*Shuo Yang,Zheyu Zhang,Bardh Prenkaj,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SAGE 是一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的新型表格数据生成框架，通过引入稀疏且动态的依赖引导机制，解决现有方法在建模特征依赖时存在的密集关联和静态关系假设问题。该方法将特征离散化为值感知伪特征，并构建基于互信息的稀疏依赖图，通过显式上下文选择或隐式对数修正来指导生成过程，使 LLM 能够聚焦于真正相关的信息。实验表明，SAGE 在六个数据集上显著提升了数据保真度与下游任务性能，F1 分数提升 10%，同时降低政策违规风险，验证了自适应结构在表格生成中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 LLM 的表格数据生成方法存在两个核心缺陷：一是过度密集地建模特征间依赖，引入虚假相关性；二是假设特征关系恒定不变，忽略了依赖关系随特征取值变化的动态特性。因此，亟需一种能够捕捉稀疏、动态依赖关系的新方法以提升合成数据的质量与实用性。

Method: SAGE 提出通过将特征离散化为值感知伪特征，构建基于互信息的稀疏依赖图，实现对生成过程的动态引导。该依赖图支持两种机制：显式上下文选择和隐式对数修正，从而让 LLM 只关注与当前生成相关的有效信息，避免冗余或错误关联。

Result: 在六个真实数据集上的多任务实验显示，SAGE 显著优于现有 LLM 方法，在数据保真度和下游任务性能方面均有提升，F1 分数平均提高 10%；同时减少了政策合规性违规，证明其在隐私敏感场景下的适用性。

Conclusion: SAGE 验证了在表格数据生成中引入自适应、稀疏依赖结构的重要性，为大语言模型在复杂数据合成任务中的上下文敏感控制提供了新思路，具有较高的实用价值和理论启示。

Abstract: Generating high-fidelity synthetic tabular data remains a critical challenge for enhancing data availability in privacy-sensitive and low-resource domains. Recent approaches leverage LLMs by representing table rows as sequences, yet suffer from two fundamental limitations: (1) they model feature dependencies densely, introducing spurious correlations; and (2) they assume static relationships between features, ignoring how these dependencies vary with feature values. To overcome these limitations, we introduce SAGE (Sparse Adaptive Guidance), a novel LLM-based generation framework that enforces sparse and dynamic dependency guidance. SAGE discretizes features into value-aware pseudo-features and constructs a mutual information-based sparse dependency graph. This graph adaptively guides generation through explicit context selection or implicit logit correction, enabling LLMs to focus on truly relevant information during synthesis. Our extensive experiments across six datasets and multiple tasks reveal that SAGE not only improves data fidelity and downstream utility, boosting F1 scores by 10% compared to previous LLM-based methods, but also reduces policy violations by one point. These results highlight the importance of adaptive structure in tabular data generation and provide new insights into context-sensitive control of LLMs.

We propose PathMoG, a pathway-centric modular graph neural network for multi-omics survival prediction. PathMoG reorganizes genome-scale inputs into 354 KEGG-informed pathway modules, introduces a Hierarchical Omics Modulation module to condition gene-expression representations on mutation, copy number variation, pathway, and clinical context, and uses dual-level attention to capture both intra-pathway driver signals and inter-pathway clinical relevance. Experimental results show that PED exhibits distinct correlations with traditional similarity metrics, and performs effectively in both ranking molecules for virtual screening and guiding molecular generation via reward design. ### [351] [SceneSelect: Selective Learning for Trajectory Scene Classification and Expert Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24514)
*Xinrun Wang,Deshun Xia,Ke Xu,Weijie Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种场景中心的可选择学习范式（Selective Learning），通过分析场景特征动态分配输入到最优专家模型，以解决轨迹预测中因场景异质性导致的泛化难题。核心方法SceneSelect利用无监督聚类发现潜在场景分类，并通过解耦的分类与调度模块实现高效、可扩展的模型路由，无需联合重训练即可适应新数据。在ETH-UCY、SDD和NBA三个公开数据集上均显著优于单模型与集成基线，平均提升10.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轨迹预测方法多采用单一统一模型，难以应对真实世界环境中运动速度、空间密度和交互模式的极端差异，导致泛化能力差、精度下降和计算资源浪费。

Method: 提出场景中心的可选择学习范式，通过无监督聚类提取可解释的几何与运动特征，构建隐含场景分类；设计解耦的分类与调度模块，实时将输入分配至最优专家模型，支持即插即用与免重训扩展。

Result: 在三个公开基准数据集（ETH-UCY、SDD、NBA）上，相比强基线模型，平均性能提升10.5%，验证了场景感知选择学习的有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: 传统的模型中心范式在高场景异质性下表现受限，而提出的场景中心选择学习框架通过动态路由机制显著提升了轨迹预测的准确性与泛化能力，具备良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Accurate trajectory prediction is fundamentally challenging due to high scene heterogeneity - the severe variance in motion velocity, spatial density, and interaction patterns across different real-world environments. However, most existing approaches typically train a single unified model, expecting a fixed-capacity architecture to generalize universally across all possible scenarios. This conventional model-centric paradigm is fundamentally flawed when confronting such extreme heterogeneity, inevitably leading to a severe generalization gap, degraded accuracy, and massive computational waste. To overcome this bottleneck, rather than refining restricted model-centric architectures, we propose selective learning, a novel scene-centric paradigm. It explicitly analyzes the characteristics of the underlying scene to dynamically route inputs to the most appropriate expert models. As a concrete implementation of this paradigm, we introduce SceneSelect. Specifically, SceneSelect utilizes unsupervised clustering on interpretable geometric and kinematic features to discover a latent scene taxonomy. A highly decoupled classification module is then trained to assign real-time inputs to these scene categories, and a highly extensible, plug-and-play scheduling policy automatically dispatches the trajectory sequence to the optimal expert predictor. Crucially, this decoupled design ensures excellent generalization capabilities, allowing seamless integration with different off-the-shelf models and robust adaptation across new datasets without requiring computationally expensive joint retraining. Extensive experiments on three public benchmarks (ETH-UCY, SDD, and NBA) demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms strong single-model and ensemble baselines, achieving an average improvement of 10.5%, showcasing the effectiveness of scene-aware selective learning.

### [352] [Prior-Agnostic Robust Forecast Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24517)
*Zhi Chen,Cheng Peng,Wei Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在未知状态空间下的先验无关鲁棒预测聚合问题，提出一种基于对数几率空间线性池化的简单闭式聚合规则，并在三种知识环境下给出了近乎紧致的极小极大后悔界。在条件独立信号假设下，证明了未知状态空间比已知状态空间更难，且所提方法可实现0.0255的最坏情况后悔值；在经典已知状态{0,1}设定中，后悔值低于0.0226，是首个达到此水平的显式闭式聚合器。此外，在已知专家边际分布的情况下，推广的对数几率规则在条件独立结构下实现0.0228的后悔值，下界为0.0225。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多集中于已知二元状态空间的鲁棒预测聚合，但现实场景中状态空间和先验信息常未知。本文旨在解决在完全无知（包括状态空间与先验）下的预测聚合难题，尤其关注状态值为[0,1]区间内任意实数时，相同报告概率对应不同实际频率的问题，以提升聚合器的鲁棒性与适用性。

Method: 提出基于对数几率空间的线性池化聚合规则，分析其在条件独立、黑威尔有序及一般信息结构下的极小极大后悔性能。通过理论推导建立下界，并验证所提规则在不同知识假设下的后悔上界，结合构造性证明与优化分析。

Result: 在条件独立信号下，所提规则在未知状态空间中实现0.0255的最坏情况后悔值，优于已知状态空间下的0.0226；在已知专家边际分布时，推广规则实现0.0228后悔值，下界为0.0225，表明其接近最优。

Conclusion: 本文提出的对数几率聚合规则在多种未知先验与状态空间设置下均表现出优异的鲁棒性能，首次实现了严格低于0.0226的后悔上界，拓展了鲁棒预测聚合的理论边界，具有重要的理论价值与应用潜力。

Abstract: Robust forecast aggregation combines the predictions of multiple information sources to perform well in the worst case across all possible information structures. Previous work largely focuses on settings with a known binary state space, where the state is either 0 or 1. We study prior-agnostic robust forecast aggregation in which the aggregator observes only experts' reports, yet is ignorant of both the underlying joint information structure and the full prior, including the underlying state space. Unlike the standard model that fixes the binary state space {0, 1}, we allow the (binary) unknown state values to be arbitrary numbers in [0, 1], so the same reported probability may correspond to very different realized outcome frequencies across environments.
  Our main contribution is a simple, explicit, closed-form log-odds aggregator that linearly pools forecasts in logit space, together with (nearly-)tight minimax-regret guarantees across three knowledge regimes. We first show that under conditionally independent (CI) signals, robust aggregation with an unknown state space is strictly harder than in the known-state setting by establishing a larger lower bound, and our aggregation rule can achieve a worst-case regret of 0.0255. Along the way, we also characterize tight regret bounds for Blackwell-ordered structures and for general information structures. In the classical setting with known state space {0,1}, our aggregator achieves regret strictly below 0.0226 for CI structures. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first explicit closed-form aggregator that achieves a regret upper bound strictly less than 0.0226. Finally, we extend the model where the aggregator additionally knows each expert's marginal forecast distribution; in this setting, with the CI structures, we show that a generalized log-odds rule achieves regret of 0.0228, complementing with a lower bound of 0.0225.

</details>


### [353] [A Reward-Free Viewpoint on Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24532)
*Ying-Tu Chen,Wei Hung,Bing-Shu Wu,Zhang-Wei Hong,Ping-Chun Hsieh*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多目标强化学习面临用户偏好未知的问题，传统方法依赖预设的偏好加权奖励，难以泛化到未见偏好。而奖励自由强化学习能学习适用于任意奖励函数的最优策略，因此具有天然适配多目标场景的潜力。本文旨在探索如何利用RFRL增强MORL，实现更有效的知识共享与泛化能力。

Method: 将先进的奖励自由强化学习（RFRL）算法改造用于多目标强化学习（MORL）框架；引入一个以偏好为导向的探索策略，引导智能体关注与当前偏好相关的环境区域；同时采用RFRL的训练目标作为辅助损失项，促进对多样化奖励结构的适应性学习。

Result: 在多个MO-Gymnasium基准任务上的实验结果表明，所提方法在性能和数据效率方面均显著优于当前最先进的MORL方法。消融实验验证了RFRL辅助任务与偏好探索策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究首次系统地将奖励自由强化学习（RFRL）应用于多目标强化学习（MORL），证明其在提升策略泛化能力、适应未知偏好方面的巨大潜力。该方法不仅提升了性能，还增强了学习效率，为多目标决策问题提供了一个高效且可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Many sequential decision-making tasks involve optimizing multiple conflicting objectives, requiring policies that adapt to different user preferences. In multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL), one widely studied approach} addresses this by training a single policy network conditioned on preference-weighted rewards. In this paper, we explore a novel algorithmic perspective: leveraging reward-free reinforcement learning (RFRL) for MORL. While RFRL has historically been studied independently of MORL, it learns optimal policies for any possible reward function, making it a natural fit for MORL's challenge of handling unknown user preferences. We propose using the RFRL's training objective as an auxiliary task to enhance MORL, enabling more effective knowledge sharing beyond the multi-objective reward function given at training time. To this end, we adapt a state-of-the-art RFRL algorithm to the MORL setting and introduce a preference-guided exploration strategy that focuses learning on relevant parts of the environment. Through extensive experiments and ablation studies, we demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms the state-of-the-art MORL methods across diverse MO-Gymnasium tasks, achieving superior performance and data efficiency. This work provides the first systematic adaptation of RFRL to MORL, demonstrating its potential as a scalable and empirically effective solution to multi-objective policy learning.

### [354] [Stochastic simultaneous optimistic optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24537)
*Michal Valko,Alexandra Carpentier,Rémi Munos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为StoSOO的算法，用于在噪声干扰下对函数进行全局最大化。该算法在不依赖已知半度量的情况下，通过乐观策略构建分层划分上的置信上限，自适应地选择采样点。有限时间分析表明，尽管不知道函数的局部光滑性，StoSOO的表现几乎与专门调优的最优算法相当。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: StoSOO算法采用分层分区结构，结合乐观原则构建上置信界，动态选择下一个采样点。通过递归细化搜索区域，在保证探索与利用平衡的同时，适应函数的局部光滑性质。

Result: 理论分析表明，StoSOO在有限时间内达到近似最优性能，其收敛速度接近于针对特定函数结构优化的算法，且不依赖于先验的半度量信息。

Conclusion: StoSOO是一种适用于未知局部光滑函数的鲁棒优化算法，能够在无须预先了解半度量的情况下实现高效的全局最大化，具有良好的理论保障和实用性。

Abstract: We study the problem of global maximization of a function f given a finite number of evaluations perturbed by noise. We consider a very weak assumption on the function, namely that it is locally smooth (in some precise sense) with respect to some semi-metric, around one of its global maxima. Compared to previous works on bandits in general spaces (Kleinberg et al., 2008; Bubeck et al., 2011a) our algorithm does not require the knowledge of this semi-metric. Our algorithm, StoSOO, follows an optimistic strategy to iteratively construct upper confidence bounds over the hierarchical partitions of the function domain to decide which point to sample next. A finite-time analysis of StoSOO shows that it performs almost as well as the best specifically-tuned algorithms even though the local smoothness of the function is not known.

Abstract: We consider online learning problems under a partial observability model capturing situations where the information conveyed to the learner is between full information and bandit feedback. In the simplest variant, we assume that in addition to its own loss, the learner also gets to observe losses of some other actions. The revealed losses depend on the learner's action and a directed observation system chosen by the environment. For this setting, we propose the first algorithm that enjoys near-optimal regret guarantees without having to know the observation system before selecting its actions. Along similar lines, we also define a new partial information setting that models online combinatorial optimization problems where the feedback received by the learner is between semi-bandit and full feedback. As the predictions of our first algorithm cannot be always computed efficiently in this setting, we propose another algorithm with similar properties and with the benefit of always being computationally efficient, at the price of a slightly more complicated tuning mechanism. *Vasiliy S. Usatyuk,Denis A. Sapozhnikov,Sergey I. Egorov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于噪声的谱嵌入（NBSE）方法，无需贪婪搜索即可从高维数据中选择信息丰富的特征。该方法通过构建稀疏相似性图并识别Nishimori温度β_N，利用最小特征向量捕捉度修正扩散过程的主要模式，从而自然地重新加权节点以避免中心节点主导问题。通过对数据矩阵转置并在特征空间应用NBSE，获得一维谱嵌入，揭示冗余或语义相关的维度群组，并通过均衡分箱选择每组的一个代表。证明了彩色高斯扰动对β_N的影响不超过O(σ²)，保证了对测量噪声的鲁棒性。在MobileNetV2和EfficientNet-B4的ImageNet嵌入上实验表明，即使在极端压缩下，NBSE仍能保持分类准确率：在EfficientNet-B4上仅保留30%特征时，准确率下降低于1%，优于ANOVA F检验和随机选择最多6.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有特征选择方法通常依赖贪婪搜索，效率低且易受噪声影响；同时，高维数据中的节点中心化问题（如枢纽节点主导）会影响谱分析效果。因此需要一种物理启发、无需贪婪搜索、对噪声鲁棒且能自动处理节点权重不均的特征选择框架。

Method: 构建样本间的稀疏相似性图，计算贝特定理海森矩阵的奇异点（即Nishimori温度β_N），提取其最小特征向量作为主导扩散模式，实现度修正的节点重加权；将数据矩阵转置后在特征空间应用相同流程，生成一维谱嵌入以识别冗余或语义相关维度群组；采用平衡分箱策略选出每组代表性特征。

Result: 在EfficientNet-B4上保留30%特征时，分类准确率下降低于1%，显著优于ANOVA F-test和随机选择（最高提升6.8%）；理论证明彩色高斯噪声对β_N的扰动为O(σ²)，具备强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: NBSE是一种高效、鲁棒且无需贪婪搜索的特征选择框架，能够有效识别高维数据中的冗余与语义相关特征，在极低维度压缩下仍保持优异性能，适用于大规模深度学习模型的特征精简。

Abstract: We propose Noise-Based Spectral Embedding (NBSE), a physics-informed framework for selecting informative features from high-dimensional data without greedy search. NBSE constructs a sparse similarity graph on the samples and identifies the Nishimori temperature $β_N$ the critical inverse temperature at which the Bethe Hessian becomes singular. The corresponding smallest eigenvector captures the dominant mode of an intrinsically degree-corrected diffusion process, naturally reweighting nodes to prevent hub dominance. By transposing the data matrix and applying NBSE in feature space, we obtain a one-dimensional spectral embedding that reveals groups of redundant or semantically related dimensions; balanced binning then selects one representative per group. We prove that coloured Gaussian perturbations shift $β_N$ by at most $O(\barσ^2)$, guaranteeing robustness to measurement noise. Experiments on ImageNet embeddings from MobileNetV2 and EfficientNet-B4 show that NBSE preserves classification accuracy even under aggressive compression: on EfficientNet-B4 the accuracy drop is below $1\%$ when retaining only $30\%$ of features, outperforming ANOVA $F$-test and random selection by up to $6.8\%$.

</details>


### [359] [Scalable Hyperparameter-Divergent Ensemble Training with Automatic Learning Rate Exploration for Large Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24708)
*Hailing Cheng,Tao Huang,Chen Zhu,Antonio Alonso*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HDET 是一种利用数据并行训练中多个 GPU 复制体探索学习率等超参数的方法，通过交替的‘分发’和‘收敛’阶段，在几乎无通信开销的情况下实现自适应学习率调度，并可扩展至其他标量超参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据并行训练中各 GPU 复制体执行相同更新，导致学习率配置空间未被充分利用，缺乏对超参数的系统性探索。

Method: 提出 HDET 方法，采用分发-收敛交替机制：在分发阶段各复制体使用不同学习率独立训练；在收敛阶段通过 AllReduce 平均参数。结合自动学习率控制器，利用各复制体间损失差异作为性能信号，通过无梯度元更新优化共享学习率基线。

Result: HDET 能生成自适应学习率调度，提升优化质量与泛化能力，无需额外超参数调优或增加训练预算；方法可扩展至 dropout 率、权重衰减等其他标量超参数。

Conclusion: HDET 提供了一种高效、通用且无需修改模型结构的超参数探索框架，显著提升训练效率与模型性能。

Abstract: Training large neural networks with data-parallel stochastic gradient descent allocates N GPU replicas to compute effectively identical updates -- a practice that leaves the rich space of learning rate configurations entirely unexplored during training. We propose Hyperparameter-Divergent Ensemble Training (HDET), a method that repurposes these replicas for simultaneous learning rate exploration at negligible communication overhead. HDET operates in alternating phases: a fan-out stage in which replicas train independently under a structured, symmetric spread of learning rates, and a converge stage in which parameters are averaged across all replicas via AllReduce every T steps. Building on this ensemble substrate, we further propose an automatic learning rate (auto-LR) controller that treats the relative training loss across replicas as a performance signal, updating the shared base schedule toward higher-performing configurations via a momentum-based gradient-free meta-update. The combined method produces a self-adapting learning rate schedule that improves both optimization quality and generalization without additional hyperparameter sweeps or training budget.
  Crucially, the framework generalizes beyond learning rate: any scalar hyperparameter that does not alter model architecture -- such as dropout rate, attention scale temperature, or weight-decay coefficient -- can be explored across replicas using the same fan-out/converge protocol, with inter-replica loss differences serving as zero-order hypergradients that guide the search direction. HDET is implemented as a drop-in replacement for PyTorch's OneCycleLR scheduler, requiring no changes to model architecture, optimizer, or data pipeline.

</details>


### [360] [SpecRLBench: A Benchmark for Generalization in Specification-Guided Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24729)
*Zijian Guo,İlker Işık,H. M. Sabbir Ahmad,Wenchao Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了SpecRLBench，一个用于评估基于线性时序逻辑（LTL）的规范引导强化学习方法泛化能力的基准。该基准涵盖导航和操作任务，包含静态与动态环境、多样的机器人动力学及观测模态，具有不同难度等级。通过大量实验，揭示了现有方法在复杂度增加时的局限性，并为未来更通用的方法开发提供了系统化评估平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LTL的规范引导强化学习方法在面对未见规范和多样化环境时，泛化能力尚不明确，亟需一个系统性的评估框架来分析其性能边界与挑战。

Method: 提出SpecRLBench基准，覆盖多种任务领域、环境类型、动态特性与观测模式，设计多层级难度测试场景，支持对现有方法的全面评估。

Result: 实证研究表明，现有方法在规范或环境复杂度提升时泛化性能显著下降；基准揭示了关键挑战，如状态抽象不足、规范理解偏差等，为后续研究提供方向。

Conclusion: SpecRLBench为评估和改进规范引导强化学习中的泛化能力提供了有效工具，推动该领域向更鲁棒、可迁移的方向发展。

Abstract: Specification-guided reinforcement learning (RL) provides a principled framework for encoding complex, temporally extended tasks using formal specifications such as linear temporal logic (LTL). While recent methods have shown promising results, their ability to generalize across unseen specifications and diverse environments remains insufficiently understood. In this work, we introduce SpecRLBench, a benchmark designed to evaluate the generalization capabilities of LTL-based specification-guided RL methods. The benchmark spans multiple difficulty levels across navigation and manipulation domains, incorporating both static and dynamic environments, diverse robot dynamics, and varied observation modalities. Through extensive empirical evaluation, we characterize the strengths and limitations of existing approaches and reveal the challenges that emerge as specification and environment complexity increase. SpecRLBench provides a structured platform for systematic comparison and supports the development of more generalizable specification-guided RL methods. Code is available at https://github.com/BU-DEPEND-Lab/SpecRLBench.

</details>


### [361] [Learning to Think from Multiple Thinkers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24737)
*Nirmit Joshi,Roey Magen,Nathan Srebro,Nikolaos Tsilivis,Gal Vardi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在多个思维者提供正确但可能系统性不同的链式思维（CoT）监督下的学习问题，例如不同思维者对数学问题的逐步解答或解决同一问题的不同程序执行轨迹。研究发现，在被动数据收集设置下，即使每个思维者的CoT都正确，仅使用两个或少数几个思维者的CoT监督也可能导致学习困难，这基于密码学假设。然而，文章提出一种通用的计算高效主动学习算法，该算法仅需少量每个思维者的CoT数据（与目标精度ε无关），所需思维者数量为$\log \frac{1}{\varepsilon} \log \log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}$，且被动端结果数据量为$\frac{1}{\varepsilon} \cdot \text{poly}\log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}$，即可实现有效学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在仅有最终结果监督的情况下，某些类别的学习任务难以完成；而通过单个思维者的链式思维（CoT）监督可以轻松学习这些任务。然而，当存在多个思维者且他们的解决方案虽正确但系统性不同时，如何有效利用这些多样化的CoT进行学习仍是一个挑战。本文旨在探索在多思维者CoT监督下学习的可行性，并设计高效的算法以克服潜在的学习障碍。

Method: 采用密码学假设分析被动数据收集场景下多思维者CoT监督的学习复杂性；提出一种主动学习算法，通过控制每个思维者所需的少量CoT数据、适度数量的思维者以及适量的被动端结果数据，实现高效学习。算法设计核心在于利用思维者间的多样性来提升学习效率，同时降低对高成本标注数据的依赖。

Result: 研究表明，在被动设置下，使用两个或少数几个思维者的CoT监督可能导致学习困难，这是基于密码学假设的理论结果。相反，提出的主动学习算法可在极低的每思维者CoT数据量、适中的思维者数量和合理的被动数据量条件下，实现对目标精度ε的高效学习，且其性能不随ε显著恶化。

Conclusion: 尽管多思维者提供的CoT监督在被动设置下可能带来学习难题，但通过设计合理的主动学习机制，可以充分利用思维者之间的多样性，实现高效且可扩展的学习。该研究为多视角、多解释性学习提供了理论支持与实用算法框架。

Abstract: We study learning with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) supervision from multiple thinkers, all of whom provide correct but possibly systematically different solutions, e.g., step-by-step solutions to math problems written by different thinkers, or step-by-step execution traces of different programs solving the same problem.
  We consider classes that are computationally easy to learn using CoT supervision from a single thinker, but hard to learn with only end-result supervision, i.e., without CoT (Joshi et al. 2025). We establish that, under cryptographic assumptions, learning can be hard from CoT supervision provided by two or a few different thinkers, in passive data-collection settings.
  On the other hand, we provide a generic computationally efficient active learning algorithm that learns with a small amount of CoT data per thinker that is completely independent of the target accuracy $\varepsilon$, a moderate number of thinkers that scales as $\log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}\log \log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}$, and sufficient passive end-result data that scales as $\frac{1}{\varepsilon}\cdot poly\log\frac{1}{\varepsilon}$.

</details>


### [362] [The Optimal Sample Complexity of Multiclass and List Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24749)
*Chirag Pabbaraju*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文解决了多分类学习中样本复杂度的最优依赖关系问题，证明了关于DS维度的长期猜想，确定了多分类及列表学习中样本复杂度与DS维度之间的最优关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分类学习中的样本复杂度问题长期未解，尽管已有工作提出了DS维度作为合适的复杂度参数，但上下界之间仍存在$\sqrt{\text{DS}}$的差距。

Method: 基于Hanneke等人（2026）提出的多分类假设类的新代数表征，论文引入并分析了超图密度的最大值，并证明其上界由DS维度决定。

Result: 证明了多分类假设类的最大超图密度不超过其DS维度，从而验证了Daniely和Shalev-Shwartz（2014）的猜想，确定了多分类和列表学习中样本复杂度对DS维度的最优依赖关系。

Conclusion: 本研究最终确立了多分类学习中样本复杂度与DS维度之间的最优关系，解决了该领域长期存在的理论缺口。

Abstract: While the optimal sample complexity of binary classification in terms of the VC dimension is well-established, determining the optimal sample complexity of multiclass classification has remained open. The appropriate complexity parameter for multiclass classification is the DS dimension, and despite significant efforts, a gap of $\sqrt{\text{DS}}$ has persisted between the upper and lower bounds on sample complexity.
  Recent work by Hanneke et al. (2026) shows a novel algebraic characterization of multiclass hypothesis classes in terms of their DS dimension. Building up on this, we show that the maximum hypergraph density of any multiclass hypothesis class is upper-bounded by its DS dimension. This proves a longstanding conjecture of Daniely and Shalev-Shwartz (2014). As a consequence, we determine the optimal dependence of the sample complexity on the DS dimension for multiclass as well as list learning.

</details>
